15##STEP_1####INST_1##Introduction%0A%0AIn%20the%20previous%20AI%20Car%20project,%20we%20created%20the%20auto%20navigation%20system%20using%20the%20following%20algorithm:%0A%5B-%0A%09(*)We%20first%20check%20whether%20the%20car%20can%20move%20to%20the%20cell%20on%20its%20right%20hand%20side%20(%20+js#on%20decide#+4%20).%0A%09(*)This%20cell%20must%20*1)%20not%20be%20the%20cell%20the%20car%20had%20previously%20been*%20(%20%60currentCell.right%20!=%20prevCell%60%20)%20and%20*2)%20be%20a%20road%20cell%20reachable%20from%20the%20current%20cell*%20(%20%60currentCell.reachableRoads.includes(currentCell.right)%60%20).%0A%09(*)If%20the%20car%20can't%20move%20to%20the%20right,%20we%20repeat%20the%20process%20and%20try%20to%20move%20*up*,%20*down*%20and%20to%20the%20*left*%20of%20the%20current%20cell%20(%20+js#on%20decide#+7,%20js#on%20decide#+10%20&%20js#on%20decide#+13%20).%0A%09(*)If%20there%20is%20nowhere%20for%20the%20car%20to%20go,%20we%20check%20whether%20the%20current%20cell%20is%20the%20finish%20line%20(%20+js#worked#-1%20).%0A-%5D%0A%0AIn%20this%20project,%20we%20will%20continue%20to%20improve%20the%20smart%20car%20so%20it%20can%20find%20its%20way%20on%20a%20much%20more%20complex%20map.%0A%0A(*)Once%20again,%20your%20custom%20chat-bot%20commands%20have%20been%20temporarily%20removed,%20they%20will%20be%20brought%20back%20later.##INST_1E####CODE_1####HTML##%3C!DOCTYPE%20html%3E%0D%0A%3Chtml%3E%0D%0A%3Chead%3E%0D%0A%20%20%20%20%3Clink%20href=%22https://fonts.googleapis.com/css?family=VT323%22%20rel=%22stylesheet%22%3E%0D%0A%20%20%20%20%3Clink%20href=%22/resources/css/font-awesome.min.css%22%20rel=%22stylesheet%22%3E%0D%0A%09%3Clink%20rel=%22stylesheet%22%20type=%22text/css%22%20href=%22style.css%22/%3E%0D%0A%3C/head%3E%0D%0A%3Cbody%3E%0D%0A%09%3Cdiv%20id='content'%3E%0D%0A%09%09%3Cp%20id='title'%3EAuto%20Navigation%3C/p%3E%0D%0A%0D%0A%09%09%3Cdiv%20id='grid'%3E%0D%0A%09%09%09%3Cdiv%20id='car'%3E%3C/div%3E%0D%0A%20%20%20%20%20%20%20%20%3C/div%3E%0D%0A%20%20%20%20%3C/div%
